# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5106-102">.NET Framework 中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a5106-103">本文中的表格列出 .NET Framework 4.5 和更新版本中依組件分組的已淘汰類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-104">請使用下列連結，查看每個組件中過時的成員和建議的替代做法清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-105">本主題不會列出過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-106">如需過時的型別清單，請參閱[已淘汰類型](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5106-140">系統組件中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="a5106-141">下表列出系統組件中過時的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-142">這些組件是用於以 .NET Framework 為目標的一般用途應用程式開發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-members-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5106-1139">Microsoft 組件中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1139">Obsolete Members in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1140">下表列出 Microsoft 組件中過時的成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1140">The following tables list the obsolete members in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1141">這些是特殊用途的組件，包含以個別語言 (例如 Microsoft.VisualBasic.dll) 或建置系統 (例如 Microsoft.Build.Engine.dll) 為目標的組件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1141">These are special-purpose assemblies and include assemblies that target an individual language (such as Microsoft.VisualBasic.dll) or a build system (such as Microsoft.Build.Engine.dll).</span></span>  
  
<a name="IEHost"></a>   
### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="a5106-1142">組件：IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1142">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1143">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe 組件已經從 .NET Framework 中移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1143">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1144">其所有類型和成員都已經過時，而且在 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 中不再支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1144">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1145">這些組件之前是用來裝載 Windows Form 控制項以及在 Internet Explorer 中執行可執行檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1145">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1146">這項技術的替代做法包括 ClickOnce、XAML 瀏覽器應用程式 (XBAP) 和 Microsoft Silverlight。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1146">Alternatives to this technology include ClickOnce, XAML Browser Applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>

|<xref:System.Diagnostics.SymbolStore.SymBinder?displayProperty=nameWithType>|<xref:System.Diagnostics.SymbolStore.SymBinder.GetReader%28System.Int32%2CSystem.String%2CSystem.String%29>|<span data-ttu-id="a5106-1151">建議的替代做法是 <xref:System.Diagnostics.SymbolStore.SymBinder.GetReader%28System.IntPtr%2CSystem.String%2CSystem.String%29?displayProperty=nameWithType>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1151">The recommended alternative is <xref:System.Diagnostics.SymbolStore.SymBinder.GetReader%28System.IntPtr%2CSystem.String%2CSystem.String%29?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a5106-1152"><xref:System.Diagnostics.SymbolStore.ISymbolBinder1.GetReader%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> 會接受匯入工具介面指標當做 <xref:System.IntPtr?displayProperty=nameWithType> 而不是 <xref:System.Int32?displayProperty=nameWithType>，因此可同時在 32 位元和 64 位元架構上運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a5106-1152"><xref:System.Diagnostics.SymbolStore.ISymbolBinder1.GetReader%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> takes the importer interface pointer as an <xref:System.IntPtr?displayProperty=nameWithType> instead of an <xref:System.Int32?displayProperty=nameWithType>, and thus works on both 32-bit and 64-bit architectures.</span></span>|
